)@@G@@^@)^@)^@)^@)^@)^@)^@)^@)***              OF THE FORM (N,ADDR) WHERE 'ADDNX
)@@G@@R' IS ADDRESS  *******  @H@@@9. *******              OF A TYPE TABLE OF NY
)@@G@@LENGTH 'N'                 *******  @H@@@9. *******     'RUNID' - ADDRESNZ
)@@G@@S OF RUNID DESIRED                     *******  @H@@@9. *******     'TIMOA

)@@G@@***              FORMAT)                                       *******  OC
)@@G@@@H@@@9. *******     'WD#' - WORD # IN LOG ENTRY TO BE COMPARED AGAINST  OD
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. *******             KEY FOR MATCH.  IF 0, THE WHOLE OE
)@@G@@ENTRY IS       *******  @H@@@9. *******             SEARCHED FOR A STRINOF
)@@G@@G MATCH WITH KEY.          *******  @H@@@9. *******     'KEY' - ADDRESS OG

)@@G@@                           *******  @H@9@8. *******       'TIME' IS STARON
)@@G@@T TIME OF SEARCH (TDATE$)              *******  @H@9@8. *******       'WOO
)@@G@@D #' IS WORD NO. IN BUFFER WHICH IS TO             *******  @H@9@8. ****OP
)@@G@@***              BE USED AS A SEARCH KEY                       *******  OQ
)@@G@@@H@9@8. *******       'KEY'  IS KEY TO BE USED                          OR
)@@G@@   *******  @H@9@8. *******       'BUFFER' IS OUTPUT BUFFER             OS
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. *******                                 OT
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@9@8. ******* 'BUFFER' = 0 IF LOG OU
)@@G@@FINISHED OR ERROR                      *******  @H@@@9. ******* 'BUFFER'OV
)@@G@@ = 0 IF LOG FINISHED OR ERROR.                     *******  @H@@@9. ****OW
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  OX
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ******* WHENEVER A NEW BLOCK IS READ, THE EXTERNAL TAG 'NEWBLOCKOY
)@@G@@'  *******  @H@@@8. ******* WILL = 1.                                   OZ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. *******                                 PA
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@9. ******* IF USER WISHES TO SKPB
)@@G@@IP REST OF CURRENT BLOCK, THE EXTERNAL *******  @H@@@9. ******* 'ENTRYNUPC

)@@G@@***                                                            *******  PE

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. ******* WILL READ THAT FILE RATHER THAN CURRENT SYSTPG
)@@G@@EM MASTER LOG  *******  @H@@@9. ******* FILE ON MASS STORAGE.           PH
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. *******                     PI
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@9. ******* IF EXTERPJ
)@@G@@NAL TAG 'PRINTCYCLE' IS SET, A SUMMARY             *******  @H@@@9. ****PK
)@@G@@*** LINE IS PRINTED FOR EACH CYCLE OF THE SYSTEM MASTER LOG    *******  PL
)@@G@@@H@@@9. ******* FILE SCANNED.                                           PM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@9. *******                                             PN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. ******* COUNTS OF THE NUMBER OF BLOCKS APO
)@@G@@ND THE NUMBER OF RECORDS   *******  @H@@@9. ******* ARE MAINTAINED IN EXPP
)@@G@@TERNAL TAGS 'NBLOCKS' AND 'NRECS'.     *******  @H@@@9. *******         PQ
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****PR
)@@G@@*** THIS SUBROUTINE IS COMPATIBLE WITH FORTRAN V AND           *******  PS
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ******* ASCII FORTRAN.                                          PT
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******                                             PU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@9. ******* THE 'BYTESUB' SUBROUTINES ARE REPV
)@@G@@FERENCED.                  *******  @H@@@9. *******                     PW
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* REVISIONPX
)@@G@@ SUMMARY                                           *******  @H@@@8. ****PY
)@@G@@*** ----------------                                           *******  PZ
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         QA
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R1  - FIRST RELEASE                        QB
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ******* 1R2  - REMOVE TAPE LOGIC AND REPQC

)@@G@@        . CLEAR FIRST TIME THRU FLAG@D@@@8          J         EXIT      TA

)@@G@@  . GET LOG TIME  @E@@@8          SLJ       DTDATE            . COMPARE TE
)@@G@@WITH STIME  @G@9@8          AU        A2,60*60          . IF STIME MORE TF
)@@G@@THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@9          AU,U      A2,60*60          . IF STIMETG

)@@G@@FUTURE, SKIP REST OF BLOCK    @G@9@8          SZ        NBUF            TI
)@@G@@  . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRYNUM  TJ
)@@G@@        . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @F@9@8          JN        A2,CTK
)@@G@@ONT1          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @F@@@9          JN        A2,CTL
)@@G@@ONT2          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @E@@@9CONT3     TZ        PRIVTM
)@@G@@              . IS RUN PRIVILEGED?  @C@@@9          J         CONT4     TN
)@@G@@        . YES     @F@@@9          L         A0,('EXEC 8')     . NO, SKIPTO

)@@G@@EY IF SPECIFIED   @G@@@9CONT9     L         A0,KEY            . CHECK SEUS
)@@G@@ARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @ @9@8          JZ        A0,CONT6  @ @@@9      UT
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,CONT10 @D@@@9          TZ        WDNO              . ISUU
)@@G@@ WORD # = 0?@G@@@9          J         CONT9A            . NO, PLAIN SEARUV

)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         EXIT              . RETURN  @I@9@8CONT7     TNVK
)@@G@@Z       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FILE, FINISHED     VL
)@@G@@@I@@@9CONT11    TNZ       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FVM
)@@G@@ILE, FINISHED     @E@9@8          LMJ       X11,NEXT          . GET NEXTVN

)@@G@@        . FOR V   @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. **********************************VU

)@@G@@****************************************************************  @[@@@8VX
)@@G@@.     @]@@@8READ      . @F@9@8          TZ        NBUF              . ISVY
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @F@@@9          TZ        ENTRYNUM          . ISVZ
)@@G@@ NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @B@@@8          J         READ3             . NOWA
)@@G@@@I@@@8          L         A0,READP+5        . YES, INCREMENT DRUM ADDRESWB
)@@G@@S BY 8 SECTORS    @^@@@8          A,U       A0,8@ @@@8READ1     S       WC
)@@G@@  A0,READP+5@F@@@8          IOW$      READP             . READ NEXT 224 WD
)@@G@@WORD BLOCK  @ @@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3   @C@@@8          J       WE
)@@G@@  READE             . ERROR   @F@@@9          INC       NBLOCKS         WF
)@@G@@  . INCREMENT BLOCK COUNT     @#@@@9          NOP     @E@@@8          L WG
)@@G@@        A0,('SYSLOG')     . LOG FILE HEADER ?   @ @@@8          TE      WH
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @B@@@8          J         READ2             . NO@G@@@8      WI
)@@G@@    L         A0,BUFFER+2       . YES, GET SECTOR ADDRESS OF DATA @G@@@9WJ
)@@G@@          A         A0,READP+5        . ADD TO PRESENT SECTOR ADDRESS   WK
)@@G@@@G@@@8          J         READ1             . GO BACK AND READ THAT SECTWL
)@@G@@OR    @F@@@8READ2     L,S6      A0,BUFFER         . SET MAX NO. OF BUFFEWM
)@@G@@RS    @G@@@8          JZ        A0,READ           . SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO WN
)@@G@@ENTRIES     @ @@@8          S         A0,MNBUF  @F@9@8          L,U     WO
)@@G@@  A0,1              . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@F@@@9          SP1     WP
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG@A@9@8          S       WQ
)@@G@@  A0,NEWBLOCK     @^@@@8          J         $+2 @G@@@8READ3     SZ      WR
)@@G@@  NEWBLOCK          . CLEAR NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAG    @F@9@8          L WS
)@@G@@        A0,NBUF           . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @F@@@9          L WT
)@@G@@        A0,ENTRYNUM       . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFFERS  @^@@@8          AUWU
)@@G@@,U      A0,1@ @@@8          MSI,U     A0,28     @ @@@8          A,U     WV
)@@G@@  A0,BUFFER @ @@@8          S         A0,X5     @F@@@8          TG      WW
)@@G@@  A1,MNBUF          . IF = MNBUF, RESET TO 0    @^@@@8          SZ      WX
)@@G@@  A1  @ @9@8          S         A1,NBUF   @A@@@9          S         A1,EWY
)@@G@@NTRYNUM     @C@9@8          J         0,X11             . RETURN  @F@@@9WZ
)@@G@@          INC       NRECS             . INCREMENT NO. OF RECORDS  @#@@@9XA
)@@G@@          NOP     @C@@@9          J         0,X9              . RETURN  XB
)@@G@@@F@@@8READE     .                           . CLEAN END-OF-FILE CHECK   XC
)@@G@@@E@@@8          L,S1      A0,READP+3        . CHECK FOR 1ST EOF   @^@@@8XD
)@@G@@          TE,U      A0,1@F@@@8          J         EXIT              . NOXE
)@@G@@T EOF, OTHER I/O ERROR  @E@@@8          IOW$      READP             . REXF
)@@G@@AD NEXT RECORD    @D@@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3           . I/O ERROXG
)@@G@@R?    @F@@@8          J         EXIT              . YES, PROBABLY DOUBLEXH
)@@G@@ EOF  @F@@@8          L,H2      A0,READP+3        . CHECK IF 14 WD BUFFEXI
)@@G@@R READ@ @@@8          TE,U      A0,14     @E@@@8          J         EXITXJ
)@@G@@              . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8          L         A0,(054160XK
)@@G@@0000000) . CHECK FOR END-OF-TAPE SDF LABEL@ @@@8          TE        A0,BXL
)@@G@@UFFER @E@@@8          J         EXIT              . NO, GARBAGE READ    XM
)@@G@@@G@@@8          TSWAP$    FACPKT            . CLEAN END-OF-REEL, SWAP TAXN
)@@G@@PES   @^@@@8          J         READ@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************XO
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@8. ****XP
)@@G@@******           GET NEXT LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE                 *******  XQ
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************XR
)@@G@@**********  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8NEXT      . @D@9@8          CSF$      FREEXS
)@@G@@,NFREE        . @FREE MASTER  @D@@@9          CSF$      FREE,NFREE      XT
)@@G@@  . @FREE LOG$    @E@9@8          L,S3      A1,CYCLE          . IS CYCLEXU
)@@G@@ = -0 ?     @E@@@9NEXTA     INC       LOGCYCLE          . INCREMENT LOGCXV
)@@G@@YCLE  @D@9@8NEXTA     TNE,U     A1,'0'            . IF SO, ERROR  @F@@@9XW
)@@G@@          J         0,X9              . IF LOGCYCLE WAS 0, ERROR  @ @9@8XX
)@@G@@          J         0,X11     @D@9@8          AN,U      A1,1            XY
)@@G@@  . UPDATE CYCLE  @ @9@8          S,S3      A1,CYCLE  @E@'@9          E$XZ
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  @^@'@9          E$MSG   YA
)@@G@@  USE @A@'@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     @A@@@'          L       YB
)@@G@@  A5,LOGCYCLE     @^@'@9          A,U       A0,1@^@@@'          A,U     YC
)@@G@@  A5,1@ @@@'          L,U       A6,' '    @E@@@'          SLJ       CYCLYD
)@@G@@E             . ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE   @#@;@9          E$DECV  @#@;@9      YE
)@@G@@    E$MSGR  @G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE          . @USE MASTER,SYYF
)@@G@@S$*SYSTEM$...     @F@;@9          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . @USE LOGYG
)@@G@@$,SYS$*SYSTEM$... @D@9@8          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A MYH
)@@G@@ASTER @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG          . @ASG,A LOG$   @E@@@8YI
)@@G@@          JN        A0,NEXTA          . NG, TRY NEXT CYCLE  @H@@@9      YJ
)@@G@@    TNZ       PRINTCYCLE        . DOES USER WANT MASTER LOG SUMMARY?    YK
)@@G@@@B@@@9          J         NEXTB             . NO@G@@@9          MSCON$  YL
)@@G@@  MSCONPKT          . YES, GET MAIN ITEM FOR LOG FILE @E@@@9          E$YM
)@@G@@DIT     EPKT              . INITIATE EDITOR     @D@@@9          E$FD2   YN
)@@G@@  BUFFER+1          . QUALIFIER     @^@@@9          E$CHAR    '*' @D@@@9YO
)@@G@@          E$FD2     BUFFER+3          . FILE-NAME     @^@@@9          E$YP
)@@G@@CHAR    '(' @D@@@9          E$DECV    BUFFER+17,,T3     . ABS CYCLE     YQ
)@@G@@@^@@@9          E$MSG     MESS@A@@@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     YR
)@@G@@@^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@D@@@9          E$DECV                    YS
)@@G@@  . REL CYCLE     @#@@@9          E$MSGR  @E@@@9          E$DAY3    BUFFYT
)@@G@@ER+19         . CATALOGUE TDATE     @^@@@9          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@9YU
)@@G@@          E$TIME    BUFFER+19 @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1           YV
)@@G@@  . SKIP A LINE   @E@@@9          E$PRINT                     . PRINT SUYW
)@@G@@MMARY LINE  @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   YX
)@@G@@@G@@@'NEXTB     TNZ       STIME             . WAS A START TIME SPECIFIEDYY
)@@G@@?     @B@;@'          J         NEXTX             . NO@B@@@;          J YZ
)@@G@@        NEXTC             . NO@F@@@'          A,U       A5,1            ZA
)@@G@@  . YES, ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE +1 @E@@@'          L,U       A6,'1'          ZB
)@@G@@  .   FOR LOOK AHEAD    @ @@@'          SLJ       CYCLE     @H@@@'      ZC
)@@G@@    JN        A0,NEXTC          . PROBLEM WITH THAT CYCLE, FORGET IT    ZD
)@@G@@@F@@@'          MSCON$    MSCONPKT1         . GET MAIN ITEM OF CYCLE    ZE
)@@G@@@G@@@'          L         A0,STIME          . COMPARE START TIME WITH CYZF
)@@G@@CLE'S @E@@@'          L         A1,BUFFER+19      .    CATALOGUE TIME   ZG
)@@G@@@H@@@'          SLJ       DTDATE            . IF START TIME > CATALOGUE ZH
)@@G@@TIME, SKIP  @E@;@'          JN        A2,NEXTA          .    PRESENT CYCZI
)@@G@@LE    @E@@@;          JN        A2,NEXT           .    PRESENT CYCLE    ZJ
)@@G@@@F@9@8          LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZK
)@@G@@@F@'@9NEXTB     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZL
)@@G@@@F@@@'NEXTC     LN,U      A0,8              . INITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   ZM
)@@G@@@ @@@8          S         A0,READP+5@G@9@8          SZ        NBUF      ZN
)@@G@@        . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @G@@@9          SZ        ENTRZO
)@@G@@YNUM          . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @C@9@8          J       ZP
)@@G@@  1,X11             . RETURN  @C@@@9          J         1,X9            ZQ
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@'/.    @H@@@'. ****************************************ZR
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@'. ******* ASSIGN LOG CYCLE SUBZS
)@@G@@ROUTINE                                *******  @H@@@'. *******         ZT
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@'. ****ZU
)@@G@@*** INPUTS: A5 = REL CYCLE                                     *******  ZV
)@@G@@@H@@@'. *******         A6 = LOG$ SUFFIX                                ZW
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@'. *******                                             ZX
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@'. ****************************************ZY
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@'CYCLE     +         0   @E@@@'ZZ
)@@G@@          E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'USE' IMAGE    @D@@@'      AA
)@@G@@    E$MSG     USE               . '@USE LOG$&'  @D@@@'          E$FD1   AB
)@@G@@  A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @C@@@'          E$MSGR              AC
)@@G@@        . ',(&'   @D@@@'          E$DECV    A5                . REL CYCLAD
)@@G@@E     @ @@@'          E$MSGR    . ')'     @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFAE
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . SUBMIT USE IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$DIT     EPKT      AF
)@@G@@        . EDIT 'ASG' IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$MSG     ASG             AG
)@@G@@  . '@ASG,AI LOG$&'     @D@@@'          E$FD1     A6                . LOAH
)@@G@@G$ SUFFIX   @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . SUBMIT ASG IMAAI
)@@G@@GE    @C@@@'          J         *CYCLE            . RETURN  @[@@@'.     AJ
)@@G@@@[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************************************************AK
)@@G@@*********************** @H@@@8. *******                                 AL
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. ******* TDATE TIME DIFFERENCAM
)@@G@@E SUBROUTINE                           *******  @H@@@8. *******         AN
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****AO
)@@G@@*** WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 10/07/77                            *******  AP
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         AQ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* THIS SUBROUTINE WILL CALCULATE THE TIME DIFFAR
)@@G@@ERENCE         *******  @H@@@8. ******* IN SECONDS BETWEEN TWO TIMES EXPAS
)@@G@@RESSED IN 'TDATE$' FORMAT. *******  @H@@@8. *******                     AT
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@8. ******* INPUTS AAU
)@@G@@RE IN A0 & A1 AND OUTPUT IS IN A2.  A2=A1-A0.      *******  @H@@@8. ****AV
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  AW
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************AX
)@@G@@************@#@@@8$(1)      AXR$    @E@@@8DTDATE*   +         0         AY
)@@G@@        . 'SLJ DTDATE' CALL   @D@@@8          DS        A0,DTDIN        AZ
)@@G@@  . SAVE INPUT    @H@@@8          L,H1      A2,DTDIN          . CHECK IFBA
)@@G@@ MMDDYY SAME FOR BOTH TIMES   @ @@@8          TE,H1     A2,DTDIN+1@D@@@8BB
)@@G@@          J         DTDCON1           . NO, TOO BAD   @F@@@8          L BC
)@@G@@        A2,A1             . YES, EASY CALCULATION     @ @@@8          ANBD
)@@G@@        A2,A0     @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . ALL DONEBE
)@@G@@@G@@@8DTDCON1   SLJ       DTDSUB            . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964BF
)@@G@@, D.P.@E@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP        . SAVE CONVERTED TIME BG
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         A0,DTDIN+1@G@@@8          SLJ       DTDSUB    BH
)@@G@@        . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8          AN        A0,DBI
)@@G@@TDTEMP        . CALCULATE DIFFERENCE@E@@@8          L         A2,A0     BJ
)@@G@@        . GET OUTPUT READY    @D@@@8          DL        A0,DTDIN        BK
)@@G@@  . RESTORE INPUT @C@@@8          J         *DTDATE           . DONE    BL
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************BM
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@8. ********* CONVERT TDATE$ TO SECONDS SINCE 1964      BN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************BO
)@@G@@**********************************  @^@@@8DTDSUB    +         0   @D@@@8BP
)@@G@@          S         A0,DTDTEMP+1      . SAVE INPUT    @^@@@8          SZBQ
)@@G@@        A2  @C@@@8          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMP+1      . YEAR    @ @@@8BR
)@@G@@          JZ        A3,DTDSC1 @^@@@8          AN,U      A3,1@ @@@8      BS
)@@G@@    L         A0,A3     @E@@@8          DI,U      A2,4              . CHBT
)@@G@@ECK FOR LEAP YEARS@^@@@8          A,U       A2,1@A@@@8          MSI,U   BU
)@@G@@  A2,60*60*24     @B@@@8          MSI       A0,(60*60*24*365)     @ @@@8BV
)@@G@@          A         A0,A2     @C@@@8DTDSC1    L,S1      A2,DTDTEMP+1    BW
)@@G@@  . MONTH   @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@A@@@8DTDSC2    A         A0,DBX
)@@G@@TDTAB,A2    @ @@@8          JGD       A2,DTDSC2 @C@@@8          L,S2    BY
)@@G@@  A2,DTDTEMP+1      . DAY     @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@E@@@8      BZ
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A2,60*60*24       . CONVERT TO SECS     @D@@@8          A CA
)@@G@@        A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  @G@@@8          L,S3      A3,DCB
)@@G@@TDTEMP+1       . IF LEAP YEAR AND MONTH>FEB,    @H@@@8          AND,U   CC
)@@G@@  A3,3              .    ADD AN EXTRA DAY TO CALCULATION    @ @@@8      CD
)@@G@@    JNZ       A4,DTDSC3 @A@@@8          L,S1      A3,DTDTEMP+1    @^@@@8CE
)@@G@@          TLE,U     A3,3@ @@@8          J         DTDSC3    @A@@@8      CF
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,60*60*24     @C@@@8DTDSC3    L,H2      A2,DTDTEMP+1    CG
)@@G@@  . SECS    @D@@@8          A         A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  CH
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         *DTDSUB           . RETURN  @C@9@8DTDIN     RECI
)@@G@@S       2                 . INPUT   @C@@@9DTDIN     $RES      2         CJ
)@@G@@        . INPUT   @^@9@8DTDTEMP   RES       2   @^@@@9DTDTEMP   $RES    CK
)@@G@@  2   @^@@@8DTDTAB    +         0   @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*3CL
)@@G@@1     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*28     @A@@@8          +       CM
)@@G@@  60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8      CN
)@@G@@    +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     CO
)@@G@@@A@@@8          +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*6CP
)@@G@@0*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @A@@@8          + CQ
)@@G@@        60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*30     @[@@@8CR
)@@G@@/.    @H@@@8. **********************************************************CS
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@8. **********           D A T A                  CT
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@8. **********************************CU
)@@G@@****************************************  @[@@@8.     @]@9@8$(0)      . CV

)@@G@@  . LOG BLOCK     @D@@@9BUFFER    $RES      224               . LOG BLOCDT
)@@G@@K     @ @@@8LOAD      L,S1      A0,RUNID  @ @@@8          L,S2      A0,RDU

)@@G@@RUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S3    A0,LRUNID @ @@@8          TNE,S4    A0,LDY

)@@G@@,S1   @ @9@8LLOGT     EQUF      25,X5     @ @@@9LLOGT     $EQUF     25,XEB

)@@G@@ COMMAND                               *******  @H@@@@. *******      - AHZ

)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@Q. ******** CHECK XQT OPTION $PJA
)@@G@@ROC- ISOLATES BIT CORR. TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********        JB
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@Q. ****JC
)@@G@@**** E.G.  TOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  JD
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********       TOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000000000040)              JE
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)  JF
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000JG
)@@G@@000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SOPT 'U'    =JH
)@@G@@ TOP A0,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SJI
)@@G@@OPT A2,'U' = TOP A2,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****JJ
)@@G@@****       GOPT 'U'    = ER OPT$                               *******  JK
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********                     AND A0,(000000000040)              JL
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************************************JM
)@@G@@**********************  @#@@@QP         $PROC   @^@@@QTOPT**    $NAME   JN

)@@G@@          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. **********************************JU

)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@QJX

)@@G@@$' WITH FILE$NAME(MAY BE R.J.)         *******  @H@@@Q. ****************KQ

)@@G@@EVEL    0,0,0             . RETURN TO NORMAL LEVELING @B@@@QNN        $EKW
)@@G@@QU      28*(3*(P=1)+P(1,1))   @A@@@Q          L         A0,(NN,INF)     KX
)@@G@@@ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,RINF$ @^@@@Q          J         ERR @^@@@QKY
)@@G@@          J         CONT@^@@@QINF       RES       NN  @ @@@QERR       ERKZ

)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,DUSE$ @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@QLF

)@@G@@D ESOR   *******  @H@@@Q. ********                       SUBROUTINES    LI

)@@G@@       P(1,1) =   FILE $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)                *******  @H@@@QLM
)@@G@@. ********         P(1,2) = ELEMENT $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               ***LN

)@@G@@ CALLED              *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$OR  - CALLS 'SOR'      LQ

)@@G@@) = (NWDS,ADDR)                              *******  @H@@@Q. ********  LS
)@@G@@       P(1,1),P(1,2) = ADDR,NWDS                         *******  @H@@@QLT

)@@G@@O P(0,1) , $END   @^@@@Q          J         CONT@^@@@QPARTBL**  RES     ME
)@@G@@  26  @#@@@Q          '@ASG'  @^@@@Q          $CFS(P(1,1)DL)@^@@@Q      MF

)@@G@@,3)DL)@^@@@Q          RES       8   @]@@@QCONT      . @#@@@Q          $EMH

)@@G@@P(1,1))     @ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,SOR$  @^@@@Q          ER      MK

)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,ESOR$ @^@@@Q          ER        ERR$@#@@@Q          $EMM
)@@G@@ND    @H@@@Q. **********************************************************MN
)@@G@@****************  @H@@@Q. ******* TEST FACILITY FOR MASM ELEMENTS       MO
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. *******                           MP
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ******* IF @MASM,T USEMQ
)@@G@@D, FACILITY IS PROCED ON AND IF T2 OF        *******  @H@@@Q. ******* RUMR
)@@G@@N CONDITION WORD IS = 2 (@SETC 2), SNOOPY IS TURNED ON   *******  @H@@@QMS
)@@G@@. *******                                                            ***MT
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. **********************************************************MU
)@@G@@****************  @#@@@QTEST**    $PROC   @G@@@QMASMT*    $EQU      $PARMV
)@@G@@(0)**(1*/('Z'-'T')) . TEST MODE IF @MASM,T USED @C@@@RLCN       $EQU    MW
)@@G@@  $LCN              . SAVE LC @ @@@Q          $IF       MASMT     @G@@@QMX
)@@G@@          J         CONT1             . JUMP TO ANOTHER LOCATION COUNTERMY
)@@G@@@B@@@R$(0)      '*TEST*'  . FOR IDONLY$ USE     @]@R@Q$($LCN+2)   @]@@@RMZ
)@@G@@$(LCN+2)    @^@@@QSAVE      $RES      2   @D@@@QCONT1     DS        A0,SNA
)@@G@@AVE           . SAVE A0,A1    @E@@@Q          COND$                     NB
)@@G@@  . GET CONDITION WORD  @D@@@Q          AND       A0,(0770000)      . ISNC
)@@G@@OLATE T2    @F@@@Q          TNE       A1,(020000)       . IF = 2, TURN OND
)@@G@@N SNOOPY    @^@@@Q          SLJ       TON$@D@@@Q          DL        A0,SNE
)@@G@@AVE           . RESTORE A0,A1 @H@@@Q          J         CONT2           NF
)@@G@@  . JUMP BACK TO ORIGINAL LOCATION COUNTER@#@R@Q$($LCN-2),CONT2   @#@T@RNG

)@@G@@    '      '@[@@@R$(LCN)@#@@@Q          $ENDF   @#@@@Q          $END    NI
)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $END    _@@@@@(1,1)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PNJ

)@@G@@    PRINT$    IDBUFF-3,9        . PRINT IT@D@@@E          PRINT$    0,0,FO

)@@G@@E   TNZ       PIMAGE            . HAS AN IMAGE BEEN PRINTED?@G@@@E      QI
)@@G@@    J         ERR4              . NO, ILLEGAL COMMAND AT LINE 0   @E@F@EQJ
)@@G@@          S         A2,RKEY           . SET REPLACE KEY     @E@@@F      QK
)@@G@@    SP1       RKEY              . SET REPLACE KEY     @H@@@GINSERT    TNQL
)@@G@@Z       COUNT+1           . HAVE ANY CONTROL IMAGES BEEN READ?    @G@@@GQM
)@@G@@          SLJ       INPUT             . NO, INPUT 1ST CONTROL IMAGE     QN
)@@G@@@G@@@G          NOP                         . SKIP READ USER COMMAND EXIQO
)@@G@@T     @H@F@EINSERT    TNZ       COUNT+1           . HAVE ANY CONTROL IMAQP
)@@G@@GES BEEN READ?    @G@F@E          SLJ       INPUT             . NO, INPUQQ
)@@G@@T 1ST CONTROL IMAGE     @G@F@E          NOP                         . SKQR
)@@G@@IP READ USER COMMAND EXIT     @G@F@E          TNZ       RKEY            QS
)@@G@@  . IF REPLACE KEY ON, SKIP OUTPUT  @^@G@FINSERT    TNZ       RKEY@^@@@GQT
)@@G@@          TNZ       RKEY@E@F@E          SLJ       OUTPUT            . OUQU
)@@G@@TPUT LAST IMAGE   @H@@@F          SLJ       OUTPUT            . OUTPUT LQV
)@@G@@AST IMAGE IF NOT A REPLACE    @H@G@F          SZ        A0              QW
)@@G@@  . CALCULATE # OF WORDS IN INSERT IMAGE  @H@H@GINSERTC0  SZ        A0  QX
)@@G@@              . CALCULATE # OF WORDS IN INSERT IMAGE  @H@@@H          SZQY
)@@G@@        A0                . CALCULATE # OF WORDS IN INSERT IMAGE  @ @@@FQZ
)@@G@@          L         A1,CREAD  @ @@@F          AN,U      A1,0,X7   @ @@@FRA
)@@G@@          L         X3,ASCII  @ @@@F          DI        A0,FACT,X3@^@@@FRB
)@@G@@          TZ        A1  @^@@@F          A,U       A0,1@G@@@F          L RC
)@@G@@        A2,BLANK,X3       . STORE BLANKS IN LAST WORD & NEXT@A@@@F      RD
)@@G@@    S         A2,IMAGE-1,A0   @A@@@F          S         A2,IMAGE,A0     RE
)@@G@@@G@@@F          S,S2      A0,CONTROL        . STORE WORD COUNT IN CONTRORF
)@@G@@L WORD@D@@@F          S         A0,NIMAGE         .   AND SAVE    @ @@@FRG
)@@G@@          LXM,U     X1,BUFF   @H@@@E          LXI,U     X1,1,X7         RH
)@@G@@  . BYTE # OF START OF INSERTED IMAGE     @ @@@E          L,U       X2,IRI
)@@G@@MAGE  @^@F@E          AN,U      A6,1@ @F@E          L         A0,A6     RJ
)@@G@@@ @@@F          L         A0,CREAD  @ @@@F          AN,U      A0,1,X7   RK
)@@G@@@G@F@E          SLJ       MOVE              . MOVE AND CONVERT INSERT IMRL
)@@G@@AGE   @ @@@F          S         X3,BASCII @E@@@F          LMJ       X11,RM
)@@G@@BMOVE         . MOVE INSERT IMAGE   @E@F@E          S,S2      A0,CONTROLRN
)@@G@@        . STORE WORD COUNT    @E@@@E          TZ        RKEY            RO
)@@G@@  . IS REPLACE KEY SET? @G@F@E          J         READ+1            . YERP
)@@G@@S, READ ANOTHER USER COMMAND  @C@@@F          J         INSERTC2        RQ
)@@G@@  . YES     @F@@@F          L,S2      A0,CONTROL        . GENERATE NEW CRR
)@@G@@ONTROL WORD @ @@@E          LSSL      A0,24     @D@@@E          L       RS
)@@G@@  A1,ASCII          . GET ASCII FLAG@ @@@E          A         A1,(0,1,0)RT
)@@G@@@E@@@E          TNZ       PARTBL+24         . IS OUTPUT A FILE?   @H@@@ERU
)@@G@@          A         A0,A1             . YES, ADD IN LINE SPACING AND CODRV
)@@G@@E TYPE@F@@@E          S         A0,CONTROL        . STORE DATA CONTROL WRW
)@@G@@ORD   @F@@@F          TNZ       ICKEY             . IS INSERT CONTROL KERX
)@@G@@Y SET?@B@@@F          J         INSERTC2          . NO@D@@@F          SZRY
)@@G@@        ICKEY             . YES, CLEAR KEY@F@@@FINSERTC1  TREAD$    MESSRZ
)@@G@@18,NMESS18 BUFF,END . ASK FOR CONTROL CODE@E@@@F          L,U       A0,0SA
)@@G@@,A0           . # OF WORDS INPUT    @D@@@F          JZ        A0,ERR8   SB
)@@G@@        . NO RESPONSE   @E@@@F          MSI,U     A0,6              . COSC
)@@G@@NVERT TO CHARS    @ @@@F          L,U       X1,BUFF   @ @@@F          L SD
)@@G@@        R1,A0     @ @@@F          L,U       X2,TEMP   @ @@@F          L SE
)@@G@@        R2,A0     @F@@@F          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD      . EXTRACT SF
)@@G@@USER RESPONSE     @C@@@F          J         ERR8              . ERROR   SG
)@@G@@@ @@@F          LXI       X1,A1     @F@@@F          LMJ       X11,BINT  SH
)@@G@@        . CONVERT INPUT TO BINARY   @E@@@F          J         ERR8      SI
)@@G@@        . INPUT NOT AN INTEGER@F@@@F          JZ        A2,ERR8         SJ
)@@G@@  . CONTROL CODE = 0, ILLEGAL @F@@@F          JN        A2,ERR8         SK
)@@G@@  . CONTROL CODE < 0, ILLEGAL @G@@@F          TG,U      A2,077          SL
)@@G@@  . CONTROL CODE > 076, ILLEGAL     @^@@@F          J         ERR8@H@@@FSM
)@@G@@          S,S1      A2,CONTROL        . STORE CONTROL CODE IN CONTROL WOSN
)@@G@@RD    @E@@@FINSERTC2  SLJ       PIMAGE            . PRINT NEW IMAGE     SO
)@@G@@@F@@@E          J         READ+1            . READ ANOTHER USER COMMAND SP
)@@G@@@F@F@ECHANGE    TNZ       PIMAGE            . HAS AN IMAGE BEEN PRINTED?SQ
)@@G@@@G@F@E          J         ERR4              . NO, ILLEGAL COMMAND AT LINSR
)@@G@@E 0   @E@F@E          LXI,U     X1,1,X7           . GET CHANGE CHAR     SS
)@@G@@@H@@@FCHANGE    LXI,U     X1,1,X7           . DOES COMMAND HAVE A CHANGEST
)@@G@@ STRING?    @ @@@F          L         R1,CREAD  @A@@@F          LMJ     SU
)@@G@@  X11,GETFIELD    @B@@@F          J         $+2               . NO@C@@@FSV
)@@G@@          J         CHANGEC1          . YES     @H@@@F          TNZ     SW
)@@G@@  NFROM             . WAS THERE A PREVIOUS CHANGE COMMAND?  @F@@@F      SX
)@@G@@    J         ERR7              . NO, INCOMPLETE COMMAND    @F@@@F      SY
)@@G@@    J         CHANGEC2          . YES, REPEAT LAST COMMAND  @ @F@E      SZ
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,BGET  @E@@@FCHANGEC1  LMJ       X11,BGET          . GETA
)@@G@@T CHANGE CHAR     @G@@@F          TNE,U     A0,' '            . IF IT'S TB
)@@G@@A BLANK, FORMAT ERROR   @^@@@F          J         ERR5@C@@@E          S TC
)@@G@@        A0,CCHAR          . SAVE    @G@@@E          LXI,U     X1,2,X7   TD
)@@G@@        . SEARCH FOR ANOTHER CHANGE CHAR  @ @F@E          L         R1,ATE
)@@G@@6     @ @@@F          L         R1,CREAD  @A@@@E          LMJ       X11,TF
)@@G@@BSEARCH     @F@@@E          J         ERR5              . NONE FOUND, SYTG
)@@G@@NTAX ERROR  @D@@@E          S         A2,A3             . SAVE COL FOUNDTH
)@@G@@@F@@@E          L         A0,A2             . EXTRACT 'FROM' STRING     TI
)@@G@@@ @@@E          AN,U      A0,2,X7   @G@@@E          S         A0,NFROM  TJ
)@@G@@        . SAVE # CHARS IN 'FROM' STRING   @ @@@E          L,U       X2,FTK
)@@G@@ROM   @G@F@E          SLJ       MOVE              . MOVE AND CONVERT 'FRTL
)@@G@@OM' STRING  @E@@@F          LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE 'FROM' STTM
)@@G@@RING  @F@@@E          LXI,U     X1,1,A3           . SEARCH FOR CHANGE CHTN
)@@G@@AR    @ @@@E          L         A0,CCHAR  @A@@@E          LMJ       X11,TO
)@@G@@BSEARCH     @F@@@E          J         ERR5              . NONE FOUND, SYTP
)@@G@@NTAX ERROR  @E@@@E          L         A0,A2             . EXTRACT 'TO' STQ
)@@G@@TRING @ @@@E          AN,U      A0,1,A3   @G@@@E          S         A0,NTR
)@@G@@TO            . SAVE # CHARS IN 'TO' STRING     @ @@@E          L,U     TS
)@@G@@  X2,TO     @G@F@E          SLJ       MOVE              . MOVE AND CONVETT
)@@G@@RT 'TO' STRING    @E@@@F          LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE 'TOTU
)@@G@@' STRING    @F@@@F          L         A1,X1             . SEE IF NEXT CHTV
)@@G@@AR IS AN 'A'@ @@@F          SSL       A1,18     @ @@@F          A       TW
)@@G@@  A0,A1     @ @@@F          LXI,U     X1,1,A0   @ @@@F          LMJ     TX
)@@G@@  X11,BGET  @ @@@F          TNE,U     A0,'A'    @E@@@F          SP1     TY
)@@G@@  ALLKEY            . YES, SET ALL KEY    @F@@@FCHANGEC2  TZ        PIMATZ
)@@G@@GE            . HAS AN IMAGE BEEN PRINTED?@C@@@F          J         CHANUA
)@@G@@GEALL         . YES     @E@@@F          TZ        ALLKEY            . NOUB
)@@G@@, IS ALL KEY SET? @D@@@F          J         *READ             . YES, RETUC
)@@G@@URN   @G@@@F          J         ERR4              . NO, ILLEGAL COMMAND UD
)@@G@@AT LINE 0   @G@F@E          L,U       X1,IMAGE          . SEARCH IMAGE FUE
)@@G@@OR 'FROM' STRING  @G@@@FCHANGEALL L,U       X1,IMAGE          . SEARCH IUF
)@@G@@MAGE FOR 'FROM' STRING  @ @@@E          L,U       X2,FROM   @ @@@F      UG
)@@G@@    L         R1,CREAD  @ @F@E          L,S2      A1,CONTROL@ @@@F      UH
)@@G@@    L         A1,NIMAGE @D@@@F          L         X3,ASCII          . GEUI
)@@G@@T ASCII FLAG@E@@@F          S,H1      X3,BASCII         . STORE FOR BYTEUJ
)@@G@@SUB   @ @F@E          TN        CONTROL   @ @F@E          L,T1      A1,CUK
)@@G@@ONTROL@ @F@E          L         A0,ASCII  @E@F@E          MSI       A1,FUL
)@@G@@ACT,A0        . A1=# CHARS IN IMAGE @E@@@F          MSI       A1,FACT,X3UM
)@@G@@        . A1=# CHARS IN IMAGE @ @@@E          L         A2,NFROM  @A@@@EUN
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD   @E@@@E          J         ERR6      UO
)@@G@@        . STRING NOT FOUND    @D@F@E          SSL       A0,18           UP
)@@G@@  . SAVE CHAR PT  @E@@@E          S         A0,A3             . A3=PT INUQ
)@@G@@TO IMAGE    @ @@@E          AU        A1,NTO    @ @@@E          AN      UR
)@@G@@  A2,NFROM  @E@F@E          S         A2,A6             . A6=# CHARS IN US
)@@G@@AIMAGE@E@@@F          S         A2,A6             . A6=# CHARS IN TEMP  UT
)@@G@@@H@@@E          L,U       X1,IMAGE          . MOVE 1ST PART OF IMAGE TO UU
)@@G@@ALT IMAGE   @ @F@E          L,U       X2,AIMAGE @ @@@F          L,U     UV
)@@G@@  X2,TEMP   @ @@@E          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @ @@@E          LXI     UW
)@@G@@  X2,A3     @G@@@E          L,U       X1,TO             . MOVE 'TO' IMAGUX
)@@G@@E TO ALT IMAGE    @ @@@E          L         A0,NTO    @ @@@F          SZUY
)@@G@@        BASCII    @ @@@E          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @ @@@E          AUUZ
)@@G@@        A3,A0     @ @@@E          LXI       X2,A4     @G@@@E          A VA
)@@G@@        A3,NFROM          . MOVE REST OF IMAGE TO ALT IMAGE @ @@@E      VB
)@@G@@    L,U       X1,IMAGE  @ @@@E          LXI       X1,A3     @ @@@E      VC
)@@G@@    L         A0,A1     @ @@@E          AN        A0,A3     @^@@@E      VD
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,1@ @@@F          S,H1      X3,BASCII @ @@@E          LMVE
)@@G@@J       X11,BMOVE @H@F@E          L         A1,ASCII          . CALC. # VF
)@@G@@OF WORDS IN UPDATED IMAGE     @H@@@F          SZ        A2              VG
)@@G@@  . CALC. # OF WORDS IN UPDATED IMAGE     @^@F@E          SZ        A2  VH
)@@G@@@ @@@E          L         A3,A6     @ @F@E          DI        A2,FACT,A1VI
)@@G@@@ @@@F          DI        A2,FACT,X3@^@@@E          TZ        A3  @^@@@EVJ
)@@G@@          A,U       A2,1@F@@@E          S,S2      A2,CONTROL        . STVK
)@@G@@ORE IN CONTROL WORD     @E@F@E          AN,U      A2,1              . BLVL
)@@G@@ANK OUT OLD IMAGE @E@@@F          S         X3,BASCII         . BLANK OUVM
)@@G@@T OLD IMAGE @ @@@F          L,U       X1,IMAGE  @ @@@F          L       VN
)@@G@@  A0,A6     @^@@@F          A,U       A0,6@ @@@F          LMJ       X11,VO
)@@G@@BBLANK@A@F@E          L         A3,('      ')   @ @F@E          TZ      VP
)@@G@@  ASCII     @B@F@E          L         A3,($CAS('    '))     @A@F@E      VQ
)@@G@@    S         A3,IMAGE,A2     @ @F@E          JGD       A2,$-1    @G@F@EVR
)@@G@@          L,U       X1,AIMAGE         . MOVE ALT IMAGE BACK TO ORIGINAL VS
)@@G@@@G@@@F          L,U       X1,TEMP           . MOVE ALT IMAGE BACK TO ORIVT
)@@G@@GINAL @ @@@E          L,U       X2,IMAGE  @ @@@E          L         A0,AVU
)@@G@@6     @ @@@E          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @E@@@E          SLJ       PIMAVV
)@@G@@GE            . PRINT UPDATE IMAGE  @F@@@E          J         READ+1    VW
)@@G@@        . READ NEXT USER COMMAND    @G@@@FFIND      L,U       X3,FINDKEYVX
)@@G@@        . POINT TO POINT TO FIND DATA     @ @@@F          L,U       X4,NVY
)@@G@@FIMAGE@F@@@FFINDC1    L         A6,CREAD          . BYTE # OF END OF INPVZ
)@@G@@UT    @F@@@FFINDL     AN,U      A6,1              . FIND LAST NON-BLANK WA
)@@G@@CHAR  @ @@@F          LXI       X1,A6     @ @@@F          LMJ       X11,WB
)@@G@@BGET  @ @@@F          TNE,U     A0,' '    @ @@@F          J         FINDWC
)@@G@@L     @F@@@F          JNZ       A6,FINDC2         . IS A STRING SPECIFIEWD
)@@G@@D?    @H@@@F          TNZ       0,X4              . NO, WAS THERE A PREVWE
)@@G@@IOUS COMMAND?     @F@@@F          J         ERR7              . NO, INCOWF
)@@G@@MPLETE COMMAND    @F@@@F          SP1       0,X3              . YES, SETWG
)@@G@@ FIND/LOCATE KEY  @F@@@F          J         *READ             . REPEAT PWH
)@@G@@REVIOUS COMMAND   @G@@@FFINDC2    AN        A6,X7             . A6=# CHAWI
)@@G@@RS IN FIND/LOC IMAGE    @ @@@F          LXI,U     X1,1,X7   @ @@@F      WJ
)@@G@@    L,U       X2,1,X4   @ @@@F          L         A0,A6     @G@@@F      WK
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE STRING TO FIND/LOC IMAGE   @E@@@FWL
)@@G@@          S         A0,0,X4           . SAVE # OF CHARS     @E@@@F      WM
)@@G@@    SP1       0,X3              . SET FIND/LOCATE KEY @C@@@F          J WN
)@@G@@        *READ             . EXIT    @G@@@FFINDCHK   L,U       X1,IMAGE  WO
)@@G@@        . COMPARE IMAGE TO FIND IMAGE     @ @@@F          L,U       X2,FWP
)@@G@@IMAGE @D@@@F          L         X3,ASCII          . GET ASCII KEY @E@@@FWQ
)@@G@@          S,H1      X3,BASCII         . STORE FOR BYTESUB   @ @@@F      WR
)@@G@@    L         A0,NFIMAGE@ @@@F          LMJ       X11,BCOMP @E@@@F      WS
)@@G@@    JNZ       A0,*READ          . IF NO COMPARE, EXIT @E@@@F          SLWT
)@@G@@J       PIMAGE            . PRINT IMAGE FOUND   @D@@@F          SZ      WU
)@@G@@  FINDKEY           . CLEAR FIND KEY@F@@@F          J         READ+1    WV
)@@G@@        . READ NEXT USER COMMAND    @E@@@FLOCATE    L,U       X3,LOCKEY WW
)@@G@@        . PT TO LOCATE DATA   @ @@@F          L,U       X4,NLIMAGE@E@@@FWX
)@@G@@          J         FINDC1            . SAME AS FIND LOGIC  @H@@@FLOCCHKWY
)@@G@@    L,U       X1,IMAGE          . SEARCH FOR LOCATE IMAGE IN PRESENT    WZ
)@@G@@@C@@@F          L,U       X2,LIMAGE         .   IMAGE @E@@@F          L XA
)@@G@@        A1,NIMAGE         . # OF WORDS IN IMAGE @D@@@F          L       XB
)@@G@@  A0,ASCII          . GET ASCII KEY @E@@@F          S,H1      A0,BASCII XC
)@@G@@        . STORE FOR BYTESUB   @F@@@F          MSI       A1,FACT,A0      XD
)@@G@@  . CONVERT WORDS TO CHARS    @ @@@F          L         A2,NLIMAGE@A@@@FXE
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD   @D@@@F          J         *READ     XF
)@@G@@        . NO FIND, EXIT @D@@@F          SLJ       PIMAGE            . PRXG
)@@G@@INT IMAGE   @E@@@F          SZ        LOCKEY            . CLEAR LOCATE KXH
)@@G@@EY    @F@@@F          J         READ+1            . READ NEXT USER COMMAXI
)@@G@@ND    @G@@@FTOP       TNZ       PARTBL+14         . IS THERE AN OUTPUT EXJ
)@@G@@LEMENT?     @G@@@F          J         TOPC              . NO, DON'T BOTHXK
)@@G@@ER WITH WARNING   @E@@@F          TREAD$    MESS15,NMESS15 BUFF,EXIT . PXL
)@@G@@RINT WARNING@F@@@F          L         A0,('Y     ')     . IF USER ANSWERXM
)@@G@@ED 'Y',     @F@@@F          TE        A0,BUFF           .   INITIALIZE EXN
)@@G@@VERYTHING   @F@@@F          J         READ+1            . OTHERWISE, IGNXO
)@@G@@ORE COMMAND @D@@@FTOPC      L,U       X1,NCOUNT-1       . CLEAR COUNTS  XP
)@@G@@@ @@@F          SZ        COUNT,X1  @ @@@F          JGD       X1,$-1    XQ
)@@G@@@D@@@F          L,U       X1,NKEYS-1        . CLEAR KEYS    @ @@@F      XR
)@@G@@    SZ        KEYS,X1   @ @@@F          JGD       X1,$-1    @E@@@F      XS
)@@G@@    PRINT$    MESS16,NMESS16    . PRINT 'TOP' MESSAGE @E@@@F          J XT
)@@G@@        INIT              . GO TO INITIALIZATION@A@@@FPRINT     L,U     XU
)@@G@@  X3,PRINTKEY     @F@@@F          SLJ       NINT              . PROCESS XV
)@@G@@INTEGER FIELD     @C@@@F          J         *READ             . RETURN  XW
)@@G@@@ @@@FNEXT      L,U       X3,NEXTKEY@F@@@F          SLJ       NINT      XX
)@@G@@        . PROCESS INTEGER FIELD     @C@@@F          J         *READ     XY
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @F@@@FGO        L,U       X3,NEXTKEY        . PROCESS XZ
)@@G@@INTEGER FIELD     @H@@@F          SLJ       NINT              .    USINGYA
)@@G@@ SAME KEY AS NEXT COMMAND     @I@@@F          L         A0,NEXTKEY      YB
)@@G@@  . CALC LINE NUMBER DIFFERENCE FROM CURRENT    @ @@@F          AN      YC
)@@G@@  A0,LINENO @E@@@F          S         A0,NEXTKEY        . STORE AS NEXT YD
)@@G@@KEY   @F@@@F          JP        A0,*READ          . RETURN IF FORWARD INYE
)@@G@@ FILE @G@@@F          PRINT$    MESS20,NMESS20    . IF BACKWARD, PRINT DYF
)@@G@@IAGNOSTIC   @D@@@F          SZ        NEXTKEY           . CLEAR NEXT KEYYG
)@@G@@@F@@@F          J         READ+1            . GET NEXT USER COMMAND     YH
)@@G@@@E@@@FLINE      E$DIT     EPKT              . INITIALIZE EDITOR   @D@@@FYI
)@@G@@          E$DECV    LINENO            . LINE NUMBER   @C@@@F          E$YJ
)@@G@@PRINT                     . PRINT IT@F@@@F          J         READ+1    YK
)@@G@@        . GET NEXT USER COMMAND     @H@@@F. ****************************YL
)@@G@@**********************************************  @H@@@F. ******* PROCESS YM
)@@G@@INTEGER FIELD SUBROUTINE                           *******  @H@@@F. ****YN
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  YO
)@@G@@@^@@@FNINT      +         0   @E@@@F          SZ        0,X3            YP
)@@G@@  . CLEAR NEXT/PRINT KEY@F@@@F          LXI,U     X1,1,X7           . ISYQ
)@@G@@ THERE ANOTHER FIELD?   @ @@@F          L         R1,CREAD  @A@@@F      YR
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @E@@@F          J         *NINT           YS
)@@G@@  . NO, JUST RETURN     @F@@@F          LXI       X1,A1             . YEYT
)@@G@@S, CONVERT TO BINARY    @ @@@F          LMJ       X11,BINT  @D@@@F      YU
)@@G@@    J         ERR5              . SYNTAX ERROR  @G@@@F          AN,U    YV
)@@G@@  A2,1              . SET NEXT/PRINT KEY TO NUMBER-1  @E@@@F          JNYW
)@@G@@        A2,ERR5           . NUMBER MUST BE > 0  @ @@@F          S       YX
)@@G@@  A2,0,X3   @C@@@F          J         *NINT             . RETURN  @H@@@EYY
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************YZ
)@@G@@****  @H@@@E. ******* PRINT IMAGE SUBROUTINE                            ZA
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@E. **********************************************ZB
)@@G@@****************************  @^@@@EPIMAGE    +         0   @D@@@E      ZC
)@@G@@    TN        CONTROL           . CONTROL IMAGE?@B@@@E          J       ZD
)@@G@@  PIMAGE1           . NO@F@@@E          E$DIT     EPKT              . YEZE
)@@G@@S, EDIT CONTROL MESSAGE @ @@@E          E$MSG     MESS7     @ @@@E      ZF
)@@G@@    E$OCTF    12,CONTROL@#@@@E          E$MSGR  @F@@@E          E$PRINT ZG
)@@G@@                    . PRINT CONTROL MESSAGE     @E@@@EPIMAGE1   LXI,S2  ZH
)@@G@@  A0,CONTROL        . GET IMAGE LENGTH    @ @@@E          TN        CONTZI
)@@G@@ROL   @ @@@E          LXI,T1    A0,CONTROL@ @@@E          LXM,U     A0,IZJ
)@@G@@MAGE  @A@@@E          A         A0,(0100,0)     @F@@@E          L,S1    ZK
)@@G@@  A1,CONTROL        . IF IMAGE IS AN SDF LABEL, @G@@@E          SZ      ZL
)@@G@@  X1                .  ASSUME IMAGE IS FD.  OTHERWISE,@D@@@E          TEZM
)@@G@@,U      A1,050            .  USE ASCII KEY@ @@@E          L         X1,AZN
)@@G@@SCII  @G@F@E          L         A1,EPRINT,X1      . GET PRINT$ OR APRINTZO
)@@G@@$ INSTR     @D@@@F          EX        XPRINT,X1         . PRINT IMAGE   ZP
)@@G@@@F@F@E          S         A1,$+1            . STORE IN NEXT LOCATION    ZQ
)@@G@@@D@F@E          $-$                         . PRINT IMAGE   @C@@@E      ZR
)@@G@@    J         *PIMAGE           . RETURN  @H@@@E. **********************ZS
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@@@E. ******* OUZT
)@@G@@TPUT IMAGE SUBROUTINE                                    *******  @H@@@EZU
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************ZV
)@@G@@****  @^@@@EOUTPUT    +         0   @G@F@E          L,U       X3,3      ZW
)@@G@@        . UPDATE DATA OR CONTROL COUNTS   @G@@@F          L,U       X2,3ZX
